2:25:1401:0:14:72:387:700:12:Times:12:Times:C:Social Structure and Conflict: Evidence from Sub-Saharan Africa
2:26:1464:14:14:72:336:686:12:Times:12:Times:C:Jacob Moscona, Nathan Nunn, and James A. Robinson
2:27:1513:14:14:72:234:672:12:Times:12:Times:C:NBER Working Paper No. 24209
2:28:1541:14:14:72:136:658:12:Times:12:Times:C:January 2018
2:29:1553:14:28:72:176:644:12:Times:12:Times:C:JEL No. D74,O55,Z1
2:30:1571:28:28:273:338:616:12:Times:12:Times:C:ABSTRACT
2:31:1579:28:14:72:546:588:12:Times:12:Times:C:We  test  the  long-standing  hypothesis  that  ethnic  groups  that  are  organized  around  `segmentary 
2:32:1685:14:28:72:546:574:12:Times:12:Times:C:lineages' are  more  prone  to  conflict  and  civil  war.  Ethnographic  accounts  suggest  that  in 
2:33:1893:28:14:72:546:546:12:Times:12:Times:C:individuals  are  obligated to  come  to  the  defense  of  fellow  lineage  members  when  they  become 
2:34:1997:14:14:72:545:532:12:Times:12:Times:C:involved  in  conflicts.  As  a  consequence, small  disagreements  often  escalate  to  larger-scale 
2:35:2098:14:14:71:545:518:12:Times:12:Times:C:conflicts  involving  many  individuals.  We  test  for this  link  between  segmentary  lineage  and 
2:36:2199:14:14:72:545:504:12:Times:12:Times:C:conflict  across  145  African  ethnic  groups  in  sub-Saharan Africa.  Using  a  number  of  estimation 
2:37:2304:14:14:72:546:490:12:Times:12:Times:C:strategies, including an RD design at ethnic boundaries, we find that segmentary lineage societies 
2:38:2402:14:28:72:546:476:12:Times:12:Times:C:experience  more  conflicts  and  ones  that  are  longer  in  duration  and larger  in  scale.  We  also  find 
2:39:2617:28:28:72:346:448:12:Times:12:Times:C:Africa is only found within segmentary lineage societies.
2:40:2674:28:14:72:146:420:12:Times:12:Times:C:Jacob Moscona
2:41:2687:14:14:72:198:406:12:Times:12:Times:C:Department of Economics
